What is the date of RBSE 10th Result 2022?                The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Results may get released by the month of May 2022.                How can I check RBSE 10th Result?                Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Results can be checked through the official website i.e. rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in by entering the hall ticket there.                What is the passing score of RBSE 10th Exams 2022?                The passing score for Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Exams 2022 is 33%.                When can I apply for the RBSE 10th re-checking/re-evaluation process?                After the release of Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th results, if the student feel that they got less score then they can apply for the re-checking/re-evaluation process. The RBSE 10th Results official website is rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in and rajresults.nic.in                What are the credentials required to check the RBSE 10th Results 2022?                Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Results 2022 can be checked by entering the hall ticket number of the student. The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Results can be checked through the official website which was mentioned in the article or through our website. The Official website to check the Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Class Results 2022 is rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in.                Where can I check my RBSE 10th result 2020?                In Order To Check The RBSE 10th Result 2022, Students need to Visit The Official Website i.e. rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in. Alternatively, Students Can Also Check Their RBSE High School Result 2020 From The some of the media sites.                When and where will Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Result 2020 Marksheets will be available?                Once The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education High School Result 2020 will declared Online On Official Website, Students Will Be Provided Their Original Marksheets And Passing Certificates By Their Respective Schools. Students Are Required To Contact Their Schools In Order To Obtain Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th Result Marksheet 2020.                What is the passing mark for RBSE 10th Result 2022?                In Order To Clear The RBSE 10th Board Exam 2022, Candidates Need To Score A Minimum Of 33% Marks In Each Subject For Which They Have Appeared In The Examination. Passing Marks Are Part Of The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education Exam Policy And Leniency Is Granted To Students In This Regards.                What if I do not obtain passing marks in the Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education High School result 2022?                In Case A Student Fails To Obtain Passing Marks In The RBSE 10th Result 2022, S/He Can Appear For The RBSE 10th Supplementary Exam That Will Be Conducted In The Month Of June/July.                When will the RBSE results be announced?                RBSE has not given any information regarding the date for the results yet. The RBSE will only decide that after the lockdown is lifted. Once the date is announced, it will be available here.                How to check Rajasthan Board 10th results?                To check the results of the Rajasthan Board 10th you will have to go to the official website rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in. There you will have to click HSC (Class 10th) Examination Results -2020 or HSSC (Class 12th) Examination Results -2020. Fill in your roll number and application number in the required field and you will be able to check your result.                If you fail an RBSE 10th, will there be any supplementary exams held?                There is no information regarding this from the Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education as the answer sheets are yet to be checked. Although the RBSE will be interested in conducting supplementary exams, there are chances that students may not get enough time for Rajasthan Board 10th supplementary exams preparation. Students are advised that if they are expecting to give a Rajasthan Board 10th supplementary exam for a particular subject, they better already begin the preparations for it.                By when will the evaluation resume?                The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education (Rajasthan Board) had postponed evaluation of Rajasthan Board 10th std board exam papers due to the lockdown. It is possible that it will resume from May 3.                You can check your Rajasthan Board 10th results on these websites                Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th exam result will be available on the official website of Rajasthan Board rajeduboard.rajasthan.gov.in and rajresults.nic.in                It is unlikely that Rajasthan Board 10th results will be declared this month.                According to the previous schedule, the answer sheets were to be evaluated by this time. But as the Prime Minister has extended the lockdown till May 03 it seems unlikely that Rajasthan Board class 10th exam evaluation will be completed this month, even though the board has not given any information about this.                Do Not fall for Rajasthan Board 10th result rumours                Students and guardians are advised to only consult the official websites of the Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education for any queries and follow only the official announcements. Do not believe in rumours. The Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education has warned and has also given in writing, that it will take strict action against those who indulge in spreading rumours or misinformation.                Beware of false information about Rajasthan Board 10th results                Soon after news about the evaluation process of class Rajasthan Board 10th exams came out, some websites gave wrong information that the evaluation has started even for Rajasthan Board of Secondary Education 10th. Such fake news can cause confusion and undue stress. It is important that students be vigilant and avoid false news.
